Inspired by:
https://www.cbs.nl/nl-nl/over-ons/onderzoek-en-innovatie/project/meer-inzicht-in-mobiliteit-met-de-donutkaart
reproduced using: https://github.com/mtennekes/donutmaps/tree/main

Uses exactextract R package to ‘cut out’ mean concentrations from the
raster bricks created from the TOPAS netcdf files.

Import shape files from eurostat using eurostat R package and use the
rnaturalearth package for some countries which are missing.

![](examples/countries_shapes.png)

THe concentrations from each country are available as a raster layer

![](examples/countries_30days.png)

Loop though each label (country), here Germany is shown

![](examples/DEU_30days.png)

and cut out the mean concentration for the country area using
